RACE OVERVIEW
=============
The 2024 Formula 1 São Paulo Grand Prix, held on November 3, 2024, at the Interlagos Circuit, was a thrilling race marked by dramatic events and unexpected results. Max Verstappen of Red Bull Racing secured a remarkable victory, coming all the way from 17th on the grid after a penalty. The wet conditions played a significant role, leading to a mixed-up finishing order with Alpine drivers Esteban Ocon and Pierre Gasly claiming second and third, achieving the team's first double podium finish since 2013. Lando Norris, who started from pole position, finished in sixth place after struggling in the race. The sprint race preceding the main event saw Norris take the win.


=============
